Let‚Äôs talk about the senses of staying in the hotel first: the lobby on the first floor of the hotel is very large, and there are sofas for guests to rest and wait; the hotel facilities are relatively complete: there are restaurants, gyms, indoor swimming pools, bars, SPA spas; ruzhu rooms are large, The sound insulation effect is very good. If you compare it with the Shimao Fanxiang Hotel next door (I have also stayed in this hotel): Marco Polo Hotel is relatively expensive and suitable for leisure and family travel, while Shimao Fanxiang Hotel is more suitable for business and personal travel. The surrounding area of the hotel is worth sightseeing. In addition to enjoying the night view on the river beach, the nearby Yanjiang Avenue can visit various western-style buildings built by Western countries since the opening of Hankou as a port, and learn about the history of Wuhan's opening as a port! Of course, there is also the famous Jianghan Road Pedestrian Street nearby which is worth a visit. At the same time, all kinds of bungalows and Chinese-style buildings hidden in the surrounding streets and lanes from the late Qing Dynasty to the Republic of China are very worth visiting. There is also a bar leisure street. Sitting at a street bar and tasting wine while watching the scenery and people on the street, it is also a special experience. The inconvenience of the check-in experience is that the ordered take-out cannot be delivered to the lobby, but can only be placed in a box outside the lobby for guests to pick up. In winter, the take-out will definitely become cold outside, affecting the consumption of customers! The overall evaluation is: the hotel is worth the experience of staying.
